URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS245479437	2016-08-12 17:15:40	1605	species	Greater Sage-Grouse	Centrocercus urophasianus			3				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Churchill	US-NV-001		9			Eastgate Canyon	L2720878	P	39.2987051	-117.8664780	2014-04-11	06:15:00	obsr404509	S17876821	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	255	9.012		2	1		0	1	1		Stationary near the south end of Eastgate Canyon for 1 hour 45 minutes. Then drove NV 722 from Eastgate south and east to Carroll summit.	As we drove into a often use--over the last 30 or so years that we know of--Sage-Grouse lek site three Sage-grouse took flight from the upper end of the lek--50 to 75 yards away. They were large dark appearing birds with long pointed tails. Two appeared to be males --larger and with light breasts. They launched with heavy rapid wing beats then glided down slope to a Sagebrush covered hillside maybe 500 yards distant. After waiting for nearly 1 hour 40 minutes we walked to the upper end of the lek. There we found fresh Sage-Grouse droppings at several beat down locations and a handful of small Sage-grouse feathers spread over a 10 yard area  that we assume were dislodged during copulation.
